                  <hi rend="ital">He is of those who are knowing,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">skilful, in commerce.</hi> (A.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  It is also an epithet applied to A <hi rend="ital">blind</hi> man; (A'Obeyd, M, B;) and so <foreign lang="ar">أَبُو بَصِيرٍ</foreign>: (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">عور</foreign>:) so applied as meaning <hi rend="ital">endowed with mental perception;</hi> (B;) or as meaning <hi rend="ital">a believer;</hi> (A'Obeyd, M;) or as an epithet of good omen: (M:) and <foreign lang="ar">أَبُو بَصِيرٍ</foreign> is used as meaning <foreign lang="ar">الأَعْشَى</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">the weaksighted,</hi> &amp;c.,] for this last reason. (M.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">بَصِيرَةٌ</foreign>.    </entryFree>30:T1edb,<entryFree id="n2652" key="بَصِيرَةٌ" type="main">

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n2652-4" target="بَصَرٌ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n2645"/></foreign>, as syn. therewith, <foreign lang="ar">أَبْصَارٌ</foreign>. (B.)
